**__Jaguar Shinkansen__**
(ジャガー新幹線)
382 Parts
The Jaguar is designed to be the Shinkansen (Japanese Bullet Train) of the future. Powered by only 2 Magnetic Drives the train can accelerate from 0 to 300SPS in just over 8 seconds, however, the train must not exceed 100SPS on sharp turns. The head car (pictured) has a passenger capacity of 64 people.
